Or we have to wait for\n35: \t// tcp keepalive failing to detect a bad connection, which is at minutes level.\n36: \t// For long term streaming connections, rafthttp pkg sends application level linkHeartbeatMessage\n37: \t// to keep the connection alive.\n38: \t// For short term pipeline connections, the connection MUST be killed to avoid it being\n39: \t// put back to http pkg connection pool.\n40: \tDefaultConnReadTimeout  = 5 * time.Second\n41: \tDefaultConnWriteTimeout = 5 * time.Second\n42: \n43: \trecvBufSize = 4096\n44: \t// maxPendingProposals holds the proposals during one leader election process.\n45: \t// Generally one leader election takes at most 1 sec. ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable defined and how is it used during Raft log catch-up when a node tries to rejoin the cluster?\\n\\nHere's the complete picture of `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` and its role in Raft log catch-up:\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Definition\\n\\n`ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is defined in [`vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/storage.go`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/storage.go?L36-38):\\n\\n```go\\n// ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is returned by the Storage interface when the required\\n// snapshot is temporarily unavailable.\\nvar ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable = errors.New(\\\"snapshot is temporarily unavailable\\\")\\n```\\n\\nIt's part of the `go.etcd.io/raft/v3` library (vendored in many repos including Kubernetes and Moby).\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Role in the `Storage` Interface\\n\\nThe [`Storage.Snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/storage.go?L85-89) interface method is contractually expected to return this error when it needs more time to prepare a snapshot:\\n\\n```go\\n// Snapshot returns the most recent snapshot.\\n// If snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable,\\n// so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare\\n// snapshot and call Snapshot later.\\nSnapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error)\\n```\\n\\nThe `MemoryStorage` implementation doesn't return this error (it always has a snapshot), but real on-disk storage backends (like etcd's `etcdserver`) do — typically while a snapshot is still being serialized or flushed to disk.\\n\\n---\\n\\n## The Catch-Up Flow\\n\\nWhen a node rejoins the cluster after being down, the leader tries to replicate missing log entries via [`maybeSendAppend`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/raft.go?L616-660):\\n\\n```go\\nfunc (r *raft) maybeSendAppend(to uint64, sendIfEmpty bool) bool {\\n    pr := r.trk.Progress[to]\\n    prevIndex := pr.Next - 1\\n    prevTerm, err := r.raftLog.term(prevIndex)\\n    if err != nil {\\n        // The log probably got truncated at >= pr.Next, so we can't catch up the\\n        // follower log anymore. Send a snapshot instead.\\n        return r.maybeSendSnapshot(to, pr)\\n    }\\n    // ...\\n    ents, err = r.raftLog.entries(pr.Next, r.maxMsgSize)\\n    if err != nil { // send a snapshot if we failed to get the entries\\n        return r.maybeSendSnapshot(to, pr)\\n    }\\n    // ... send MsgApp normally\\n}\\n```\\n\\nIf the required log entries have been **compacted away** (i.e., the follower is too far behind), both the `term()` and `entries()` calls fail, and execution falls through to [`maybeSendSnapshot`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/raft.go?L662-689):\\n\\n```go\\nfunc (r *raft) maybeSendSnapshot(to uint64, pr *tracker.Progress) bool {\\n    if !pr.RecentActive {\\n        r.logger.Debugf(\\\"ignore sending snapshot to %x since it is not recently active\\\", to)\\n        return false\\n    }\\n\\n    snapshot, err := r.raftLog.snapshot()\\n    if err != nil {\\n        if err == ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable {\\n            r.logger.Debugf(\\\"%x failed to send snapshot to %x because snapshot is temporarily unavailable\\\", r.id, to)\\n            return false   // ← gracefully back off, no panic\\n        }\\n        panic(err)         // ← all other errors are fatal\\n    }\\n    // ... send MsgSnap\\n    r.send(pb.Message{To: to, Type: pb.MsgSnap, Snapshot: &snapshot})\\n    return true\\n}\\n```\\n\\n[`raftLog.snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/log.go?L291-296) first checks the in-memory unstable buffer, then delegates to the `Storage` backend:\\n\\n```go\\nfunc (l *raftLog) snapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error) {\\n    if l.unstable.snapshot != nil {\\n        return *l.unstable.snapshot, nil\\n    }\\n    return l.storage.Snapshot()   // ← may return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable\\n}\\n```\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Summary of the Catch-Up Sequence\\n\\n| Step | What happens |\\n|------|-------------|\\n| 1 | Rejoining node's `pr.Next` is behind the leader's compacted log |\\n| 2 | `maybeSendAppend` fails to fetch entries/term → calls `maybeSendSnapshot` |\\n| 3 | Leader calls `raftLog.snapshot()` → `Storage.Snapshot()` |\\n| 4 | If storage isn't ready → `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` returned |\\n| 5 | `maybeSendSnapshot` logs a debug message and returns `false` (no panic, no send) |\\n| 6 | On the next heartbeat/bcastAppend tick, the leader retries |\\n| 7 | Once the snapshot is ready, `Storage.Snapshot()` succeeds → leader sends `MsgSnap` to the rejoining node |\\n\\nThe key design point: `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is the **only non-fatal error** from `Storage.Snapshot()`. All other errors cause a panic. This gives storage backends a safe way to signal \\\"not yet\\\" without crashing the Raft state machine.\\n\\n## Sources\\n\\n- defined and how is it used during Raft log catch-up when a node tries to rejoin the cluster?\n\nHere's the complete picture of `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` and its role in Raft log catch-up:\n\n---\n\n## Definition\n\n`ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is defined in [`vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/storage.go`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/storage.go?L36-38):\n\n```go\n// ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is returned by the Storage interface when the required\n// snapshot is temporarily unavailable.\nvar ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable = errors.New(\"snapshot is temporarily unavailable\")\n```\n\nIt's part of the `go.etcd.io/raft/v3` library (vendored in many repos including Kubernetes and Moby).\n\n---\n\n## Role in the `Storage` Interface\n\nThe [`Storage.Snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/storage.go?L85-89) interface method is contractually expected to return this error when it needs more time to prepare a snapshot:\n\n```go\n// Snapshot returns the most recent snapshot.\n// If snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable,\n// so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare\n// snapshot and call Snapshot later.\nSnapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error)\n```\n\nThe `MemoryStorage` implementation doesn't return this error (it always has a snapshot), but real on-disk storage backends (like etcd's `etcdserver`) do — typically while a snapshot is still being serialized or flushed to disk.\n\n---\n\n## The Catch-Up Flow\n\nWhen a node rejoins the cluster after being down, the leader tries to replicate missing log entries via [`maybeSendAppend`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/raft.go?L616-660):\n\n```go\nfunc (r *raft) maybeSendAppend(to uint64, sendIfEmpty bool) bool {\n    pr := r.trk.Progress[to]\n    prevIndex := pr.Next - 1\n    prevTerm, err := r.raftLog.term(prevIndex)\n    if err != nil {\n        // The log probably got truncated at >= pr.Next, so we can't catch up the\n        // follower log anymore. Send a snapshot instead.\n        return r.maybeSendSnapshot(to, pr)\n    }\n    // ...\n    ents, err = r.raftLog.entries(pr.Next, r.maxMsgSize)\n    if err != nil { // send a snapshot if we failed to get the entries\n        return r.maybeSendSnapshot(to, pr)\n    }\n    // ... send MsgApp normally\n}\n```\n\nIf the required log entries have been **compacted away** (i.e., the follower is too far behind), both the `term()` and `entries()` calls fail, and execution falls through to [`maybeSendSnapshot`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/raft.go?L662-689):\n\n```go\nfunc (r *raft) maybeSendSnapshot(to uint64, pr *tracker.Progress) bool {\n    if !pr.RecentActive {\n        r.logger.Debugf(\"ignore sending snapshot to %x since it is not recently active\", to)\n        return false\n    }\n\n    snapshot, err := r.raftLog.snapshot()\n    if err != nil {\n        if err == ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable {\n            r.logger.Debugf(\"%x failed to send snapshot to %x because snapshot is temporarily unavailable\", r.id, to)\n            return false   // ← gracefully back off, no panic\n        }\n        panic(err)         // ← all other errors are fatal\n    }\n    // ... send MsgSnap\n    r.send(pb.Message{To: to, Type: pb.MsgSnap, Snapshot: &snapshot})\n    return true\n}\n```\n\n[`raftLog.snapshot()`](https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/r/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/-/blob/vendor/go.etcd.io/raft/v3/log.go?L291-296) first checks the in-memory unstable buffer, then delegates to the `Storage` backend:\n\n```go\nfunc (l *raftLog) snapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error) {\n    if l.unstable.snapshot != nil {\n        return *l.unstable.snapshot, nil\n    }\n    return l.storage.Snapshot()   // ← may return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary of the Catch-Up Sequence\n\n| Step | What happens |\n|------|-------------|\n| 1 | Rejoining node's `pr.Next` is behind the leader's compacted log |\n| 2 | `maybeSendAppend` fails to fetch entries/term → calls `maybeSendSnapshot` |\n| 3 | Leader calls `raftLog.snapshot()` → `Storage.Snapshot()` |\n| 4 | If storage isn't ready → `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` returned |\n| 5 | `maybeSendSnapshot` logs a debug message and returns `false` (no panic, no send) |\n| 6 | On the next heartbeat/bcastAppend tick, the leader retries |\n| 7 | Once the snapshot is ready, `Storage.Snapshot()` succeeds → leader sends `MsgSnap` to the rejoining node |\n\nThe key design point: `ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable` is the **only non-fatal error** from `Storage.Snapshot()`. All other errors cause a panic. This gives storage backends a safe way to signal \"not yet\" without crashing the Raft state machine.\n\n## Sources\n\n-
